It then processes special flags to extract any existing blink settings, parsing comma-separated key-value pairs from the `--blink-settings` flag and storing them in a result dictionary. Finally, it retrieves the user's preferred color scheme configuration. iterates through all darkmode settings and adds each one to the appropriate result category based on its switch name. The function filters out unset values and skips settings that haven't been modified, except for mandatory ones like the enabled flag and algorithm, which are always passed to ensure darkmode is properly activated.\n\nLooking at how settings are routed, the 'enabled' setting gets sent to `blink-settings` while all other darkmode options default to `dark-mode-settings`. {"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001","id":"msg_01E7avJpoHChRxv2ZfpMBGox","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"tool_use","id":"toolu_01ThpFxrPGWKHKQ6xyPizWtQ","name":"Write","input":{"file_path":"/workspace/regression_test.py","content":"# SPDX-License-Identifier: GPL-3.0-or-later\n\"\"\"\nRegression test for Qt 6.4 dark mode text threshold setting bug.\n\nBug Report:\n-----------\nWhen users configure the dark mode text brightness threshold setting\n(colors.webpage.darkmode.threshold.text) and qutebrowser is running with Qt version 6.4,\nthe setting has no effect on dark mode rendering.\n\nRoot Cause:\n-----------\nIn Chromium 99.0.4785.0 (which corresponds to Qt 6.4), the Chromium setting\n`TextBrightnessThreshold` was renamed to `ForegroundBrightnessThreshold`. However,\nqutebrowser is still using the old `TextBrightnessThreshold` name for Qt 6.4,\nwhich causes the setting to have no effect since Chromium doesn't recognize the\nold setting name.\n\nExpected Fix:\n-----------\nA new `qt_64` variant should be introduced that uses `ForegroundBrightnessThreshold`\ninstead of `TextBrightnessThreshold`.\n\nThis Test:\n----------\nThis regression test verifies that the text threshold setting is correctly mapped\nto the appropriate Chromium setting name for Qt 6.4. On the buggy code, this test\nwill FAIL because it incorrectly uses `TextBrightnessThreshold` instead of\n`ForegroundBrightnessThreshold`.\n\nReferences:\n-----------\n- Chromium setting rename: https://chromium-review.googlesource.com/c/chromium/src/+/3344100\n- Classifier rename: https://chromium-review.googlesource.com/c/chromium/src/+/3226389\n\"\"\"\n\nimport sys\nimport os\nimport logging\n\n# Setup path to find qutebrowser modules\nsys.path.insert(0, '/app')\n\nimport pytest\n\n# Configure logging to reduce noise\nlogging.getLogger('qutebrowser').setLevel(logging.CRITICAL)\n\n\ndef test_qt64_dark_mode_text_threshold_setting():\n    \"\"\"Test that Qt 6.4 dark mode text threshold uses correct Chromium setting name.\n\n    On Qt 6.4, the Chromium setting name changed from `TextBrightnessThreshold` to\n    `ForegroundBrightnessThreshold`. This test verifies that the threshold.text\n    configuration is mapped to the correct setting name.\n\n    This test demonstrates a regression where qutebrowser was using the old\n    `TextBrightnessThreshold` name for Qt 6.4, causing the setting to be ignored\n    by Chromium.\n    \"\"\"\n    from qutebrowser.config import config, configdata\n    from qutebrowser.utils import usertypes, version, utils\n    from qutebrowser.browser.webengine import darkmode\n    from qutebrowser.misc import objects\n\n    # Initialize config\n    configdata.init(None)\n    config.instance = config.Config()\n\n    # Patch backend\n    objects.backend = usertypes.Backend.QtWebEngine\n\n    # Create Qt 6.4 version\n    qt64_versions = version.WebEngineVersions(\n        webengine=utils.VersionNumber(6, 4, 0),\n        chromium='99.0.4785.0',\n        source='test',\n    )\n\n    # Enable dark mode and set the threshold.text setting\n    config.instance.set_obj('colors.webpage.darkmode.enabled', True)\n    config.instance.set_obj('colors.webpage.darkmode.algorithm', 'brightness-rgb')\n    config.instance.set_obj('colors.webpage.darkmode.grayscale.all', True)\n    config.instance.set_obj('colors.webpage.darkmode.threshold.text', 100)\n\n    # Get the dark mode settings that would be passed to Chromium\n    darkmode_settings = darkmode.settings(versions=qt64_versions, special_flags=[])\n\n    # Extract the dark-mode-settings which should contain the threshold setting\n    dark_mode_settings_list = darkmode_settings.get('dark-mode-settings', [])\n\n    # Find the threshold setting in the returned settings\n    threshold_setting = None\n    for key, value in dark_mode_settings_list:\n        if 'Threshold' in key and 'Foreground' not in key:\n            # Found the old (buggy) setting name\n            threshold_setting = (key, value)\n            break\n\n    # Also check for the correct setting name\n    foreground_setting = None\n    for key, value in dark_mode_settings_list:\n        if key == 'ForegroundBrightnessThreshold':\n            foreground_setting = (key, value)\n            break\n\n    # Print debug information\n    print(f\"\\nDarkmode settings: {darkmode_settings}\")\n    print(f\"Dark-mode-settings list: {dark_mode_settings_list}\")\n    print(f\"Threshold setting found: {threshold_setting}\")\n    print(f\"Foreground setting found: {foreground_setting}\")\n\n    # This assertion will FAIL on the buggy code because:\n    # - The buggy code uses the old variant (qt_63) which has 'TextBrightnessThreshold'\n    # - The fixed code should use a new variant (qt_64) which has 'ForegroundBrightnessThreshold'\n    #\n    # Expected behavior (after fix):\n    # - foreground_setting should be ('ForegroundBrightnessThreshold', '100')\n    # - threshold_setting should be None\n    #\n    # Buggy behavior (current):\n    # - foreground_setting is None\n    # - threshold_setting is ('TextBrightnessThreshold', '100')\n\n    # Verify that the threshold.text setting is present\n    assert threshold_setting is not None or foreground_setting is not None, (\n        \"Dark mode text threshold setting is missing entirely from dark-mode-settings. \"\n        \"Expected either 'TextBrightnessThreshold' (old) or 'ForegroundBrightnessThreshold' (correct).\"\n    )\n\n    # Verify the CORRECT setting name is used for Qt 6.4\n    assert foreground_setting is not None, (\n        f\"Qt 6.4 should use 'ForegroundBrightnessThreshold' (Chromium 99.0.4785+), \"\n        f\"not 'TextBrightnessThreshold' (older Chromium versions). \"\n        f\"Found settings: {dark_mode_settings_list}. \"\n        f\"This is a regression test for the bug where threshold.text setting was ignored on Qt 6.4.\"\n    )\n\n    # Verify the setting has the correct value\n    assert foreground_setting[1] == '100', (\n        f\"Expected threshold value of '100', but got '{foreground_setting[1]}'\"\n    )\n\n    # Verify the OLD setting name is NOT used for Qt 6.4\n    assert threshold_setting is None, (\n        f\"Qt 6.4 should NOT use the old 'TextBrightnessThreshold' setting. \"\n        f\"Found: {threshold_setting}. The setting should be renamed to 'ForegroundBrightnessThreshold'. \"\n        f\"This is causing the threshold.text configuration to be ignored by Chromium.\"\n    )\n\n\nif __name__ == '__main__':\n    # Run the test directly\n    test_qt64_dark_mode_text_threshold_setting()\n    print(\"\\n✓ Test passed! However,\nqutebrowser is still using the old `TextBrightnessThreshold` name for Qt 6.4,\nwhich causes the setting to have no effect since Chromium doesn't recognize the\nold setting name.\n\nExpected Fix:\n-----------\nA new `qt_64` variant should be introduced that uses `ForegroundBrightnessThreshold`\ninstead of `TextBrightnessThreshold`.\n\nThis Test:\n----------\nThis regression test verifies that the text threshold setting is correctly mapped\nto the appropriate Chromium setting name for Qt 6.4. Initialize config\n    configdata.init(None)\n    config.instance = config.Config()\n\n    # Patch backend\n    objects.backend = usertypes.Backend.QtWebEngine\n\n    # Create Qt 6.4 version\n    qt64_versions = version.WebEngineVersions(\n        webengine=utils.VersionNumber(6, 4, 0),\n        chromium='99.0.4785.0',\n        source='test',\n    )\n\n    # Enable dark mode and set the threshold.text setting\n    config.instance.set_obj('colors.webpage.darkmode.enabled', True)\n    config.instance.set_obj('colors.webpage.darkmode.algorithm', 'brightness-rgb')\n    config.instance.set_obj('colors.webpage.darkmode.grayscale.all', True)\n    config.instance.set_obj('colors.webpage.darkmode.threshold.text', 100)\n\n    # Find the threshold setting in the returned settings\n    threshold_setting = None\n    for key, value in dark_mode_settings_list:\n        if 'Threshold' in key and 'Foreground' not in key:\n            # Found the old (buggy) setting name\n            threshold_setting = (key, value)\n            break\n\n    # Also check for the correct setting name\n    foreground_setting = None\n    for key, value in dark_mode_settings_list:\n        if key == 'ForegroundBrightnessThreshold':\n            foreground_setting = (key, value)\n            break\n\n    # This assertion will FAIL on the buggy code because:\n    # - The buggy code uses the old variant (qt_63) which has 'TextBrightnessThreshold'\n    # - The fixed code should use a new variant (qt_64) which has 'ForegroundBrightnessThreshold'\n    #\n    # However,\nqutebrowser is still using the old `TextBrightnessThreshold` name for Qt 6.4,\nwhich causes the setting to have no effect since Chromium doesn't recognize the\nold setting name.\n\nExpected Fix:\n-----------\nA new `qt_64` variant should be introduced that uses `ForegroundBrightnessThreshold`\ninstead of `TextBrightnessThreshold`.\n\nThis Test:\n----------\nThis regression test verifies that the text threshold setting is correctly mapped\nto the appropriate Chromium setting name for Qt 6.4. On the buggy code, this test\nwill FAIL because it incorrectly uses `TextBrightnessThreshold` instead of\n`ForegroundBrightnessThreshold`.\n\nReferences:\n-----------\n- Chromium setting rename: https://chromium-review.googlesource.com/c/chromium/src/+/3344100\n- Classifier rename: https://chromium-review.googlesource.com/c/chromium/src/+/3226389\n\"\"\"\n\nimport sys\nimport logging\n\n# Setup path to find qutebrowser modules\nsys.path.insert(0, '/app')\n\nimport pytest\n\n# Configure logging to reduce noise\nlogging.getLogger('qutebrowser').setLevel(logging.CRITICAL)\n\n\n@pytest.fixture(autouse=True)\ndef patch_backend(monkeypatch):\n    \"\"\"Patch backend to QtWebEngine.\"\"\"\n    from qutebrowser.misc import objects\n    from qutebrowser.utils import usertypes\n    monkeypatch.setattr(objects, 'backend', usertypes.Backend.QtWebEngine)\n\n\ndef test_qt64_dark_mode_text_threshold_setting(config_stub):\n    \"\"\"Test that Qt 6.4 dark mode text threshold uses correct Chromium setting name.\n\n    On Qt 6.4, the Chromium setting name changed from `TextBrightnessThreshold` to\n    `ForegroundBrightnessThreshold`. Find the threshold setting in the returned settings\n    threshold_setting = None\n    for key, value in dark_mode_settings_list:\n        if 'Threshold' in key and 'Foreground' not in key:\n            # Found the old (buggy) setting name\n            threshold_setting = (key, value)\n            break\n\n    # Also check for the correct setting name\n    foreground_setting = None\n    for key, value in dark_mode_settings_list:\n        if key == 'ForegroundBrightnessThreshold':\n            foreground_setting = (key, value)\n            break\n\n    # Print debug information\n    print(f\"\\nDarkmode settings: {darkmode_settings}\")\n    print(f\"Dark-mode-settings list: {dark_mode_settings_list}\")\n    print(f\"Threshold setting found: {threshold_setting}\")\n    print(f\"Foreground setting found: {foreground_setting}\")\n\n    # Expected behavior (after fix):\n    # - foreground_setting should be ('ForegroundBrightnessThreshold', '100')\n    # - threshold_setting should be None\n    #\n    # Buggy behavior (current):\n    # - foreground_setting is None\n    # - threshold_setting is ('TextBrightnessThreshold', '100')\n\n    # Verify that the threshold.text setting is present\n    assert threshold_setting is not None or foreground_setting is not None, (\n        \"Dark mode text threshold setting is missing entirely from dark-mode-settings. \"\n        \"Expected either 'TextBrightnessThreshold' (old) or 'ForegroundBrightnessThreshold' (correct).\"\n    )\n\n    # Get the dark mode settings that would be passed to Chromium\n            darkmode_settings = darkmode.settings(versions=qt64_versions, special_flags=[])\n\n            # Extract the dark-mode-settings which should contain the threshold setting\n            dark_mode_settings_list = darkmode_settings.get('dark-mode-settings', [])\n\n            # Find the threshold setting in the returned settings\n            threshold_setting = None\n            for key, value in dark_mode_settings_list:\n                if 'Threshold' in key and 'Foreground' not in key:\n                    # Found the old (buggy) setting name\n                    threshold_setting = (key, value)\n                    break\n\n            # Also check for the correct setting name\n            foreground_setting = None\n            for key, value in dark_mode_settings_list:\n                if key == 'ForegroundBrightnessThreshold':\n                    foreground_setting = (key, value)\n                    break\n\n            # - foreground_setting is None\n            # - threshold_setting is ('TextBrightnessThreshold', '100')\n\n            # Verify that the threshold.text setting is present\n            assert threshold_setting is not None or foreground_setting is not None, (\n                \"Dark mode text threshold setting is missing entirely from dark-mode-settings. \"\n                \"Expected either 'TextBrightnessThreshold' (old) or 'ForegroundBrightnessThreshold' (correct).\"\n            )\n\n            # However,\nqutebrowser is still using the old `TextBrightnessThreshold` name for Qt 6.4,\nwhich causes the setting to have no effect since Chromium doesn't recognize the\nold setting name.\n\nExpected Fix:\n-----------\nA new `qt_64` variant should be introduced that uses `ForegroundBrightnessThreshold`\ninstead of `TextBrightnessThreshold`.\n\nThis Test:\n----------\nThis regression test verifies that the text threshold setting is correctly mapped\nto the appropriate Chromium setting name for Qt 6.4. Expected behavior (after fix):\n    # - foreground_setting should be ('ForegroundBrightnessThreshold', '100')\n    # - threshold_setting should be None\n    #\n    # Buggy behavior (current):\n    # - foreground_setting is None\n    # - threshold_setting is ('TextBrightnessThreshold', '100')\n\n    # Verify that the threshold.text setting is present\n    assert threshold_setting is not None or foreground_setting is not None, (\n        \"Dark mode text threshold setting is missing entirely from dark-mode-settings. \"\n        \"Expected either 'TextBrightnessThreshold' (old) or 'ForegroundBrightnessThreshold' (correct).\"\n    )\n\n    # The root cause is a breaking change in Chromium's API that renamed a Chromium setting, but qutebrowser's code still uses the old setting name for Qt 6.4.\n\n## Bug Details\n\n### Reported Issue\n- **Affected Qt Version:** Qt 6.4 (Chromium 99.0.4785.0+)\n- **Symptom:** Setting `colors.webpage.darkmode.threshold.text` to any value has no effect\n- **Scope:** Text/foreground threshold only (other dark mode settings work correctly)\n- **Status:** Confirmed in current codebase\n\n### Root Cause Analysis\n\n**Location:** `/app/qutebrowser/browser/webengine/darkmode.py`\n\nIn Chromium 99.0.4785.0 (corresponding to Qt 6.4), the Chromium setting `TextBrightnessThreshold` was renamed to `ForegroundBrightnessThreshold`.\n\nThe qutebrowser code currently:\n1. Defines three variants: `qt_515_2`, `qt_515_3`, and `qt_63`\n2. No separate `qt_64` variant exists\n3. Qt 6.4 falls through to the `qt_63` variant (because `6.4 >= 6.3`)\n4. The `qt_63` variant uses the old setting name: `TextBrightnessThreshold`\n5. Chromium 99.0.4785.0+ doesn't recognize this old setting name, so it's ignored\n\n**Evidence from Code Review:**\n\n```python\n# darkmode.py line 279-281 (current code)\n_DEFINITIONS[Variant.qt_63] = _DEFINITIONS[Variant.qt_515_3].copy_add_setting(\n    _Setting('increase_text_contrast', 'IncreaseTextContrast', _INT_BOOLS),\n)\n```\n\nThe qt_63 definition only adds one setting (increase_text_contrast) but doesn't change the threshold setting name. The threshold setting still uses the old name from qt_515_3:\n\n```python\n# darkmode.py line 270\n_Setting('threshold.text', 'TextBrightnessThreshold'),\n```\n\n### Chromium Changes\n- **Rename PR:** https://chromium-review.googlesource.com/c/chromium/src/+/3344100\n- **Classifier rename PR:** https://chromium-review.googlesource.com/c/chromium/src/+/3226389\n- **Change Details:** \"Correct brightness threshold of darkmode color classifier\" and \"Rename text_classifier to foreground_classifier\"\n\n## Expected Fix\n\nA new `qt_64` variant should be introduced that uses the new setting name:\n\n```python\nVariant.qt_64 = enum.auto()\n\n_DEFINITIONS[Variant.qt_64] = _DEFINITIONS[Variant.qt_63].copy_replace_setting(\n    'threshold.text', 'ForegroundBrightnessThreshold',\n)\n\ndef _variant(versions: version.WebEngineVersions) -> Variant:\n    if versions.webengine >= utils.VersionNumber(6, 4):\n        return Variant.qt_64\n    elif versions.webengine >= utils.VersionNumber(6, 3):\n        return Variant.qt_63\n    # ... rest of the code\n```\n\n## Regression Test\n\n### Test File\n- **Location:** `/workspace/regression_test.py`\n- **Size:** 167 lines, self-contained\n- **Execution:** `python3 -m pytest -c /dev/null regression_test.py`\n\n### Test Strategy\n\nThe regression test verifies that:\n\n1. **For Qt 6.4**, the dark mode text threshold setting is configured with a value (100)\n2. **The returned Chromium settings** are examined for the threshold setting\n3. **The test FAILS on buggy code** because:\n   -
